## 1. Download data
Data downloaded from TAMUCC grid.

## 2. Proofread the decode files
818 forward reads, 818 reverse reads, but 824 listed in decode file.

## 3. Edit the decode file
Decode file edited. Some of the names had to be changed, (ex Adu-AMat_089, Adu-AMat_057, Adu-AMat_010, Adu-AMat_012) because they occured twice in the decode sheet but only once in the raw files. Names changed to reflect that these individuals were combined by the sequence facility.

## 4. Make a copy of the fq_raw files
Copying with `screen`.

## 5. Perform a renaming dry run.
Some of the original file names make it difficult to run the rename script as is, so I copied the rename script and edited it to work with all the files.

`bash renameFQGZ.bash Adu_LCWGS-TestLane_SequenceNameDecode.tsv`

writing original file names to file, origFileNames.txt...
writing newFileNames.txt...
editing newFileNames.txt...
preview of orig and new R1 file names...

## 6. Rename the files for real
`bash renameFQGZ.bash Adu_LCWGS-TestLane_SequenceNameDecode.tsv rename`

## 7. Check the quality of your data.
`sbatch /home/e1garcia/shotgun_PIRE/pire_fq_gz_processing/Multi_FASTQC.sh "fq_raw" "fqc_raw_report"  "fq.gz"`
